[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Error Location**: The overflow occurs at [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/FreeRDP/libfreerdp/crypto/[0m[95mcertificate.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m1570:14[0m[39m` within the [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`freerdp_bio_read_pem_with_policy` function. This is a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte write operation that [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexceeds the allocated buffer boundary.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Call Stack Analysis**: The vulnerability is triggered through the following [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcall chain:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfuzzer entry point[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `freerdp_certificate_data_new_from_pem`[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `freerdp_certificate_data_new_nocopy`[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `freerdp_certificate_data_load_cache`[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `freerdp_certificate_get_pem_ex`[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `freerdp_bio_read_pem_with_policy` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhere the overflow occurs[0m[1;39m)[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Memory State**: According to the shadow byte analysis, the target address [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0x502000010230[0m[39m is marked as [0m[32m'fa'[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mheap left redzone[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, indicating the write [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperation is attempting to access memory in a heap redzone area, which is a [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotected region used by ASAN to detect buffer overflows.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Access Pattern**: The address [0m[1;36m0x502000010230[0m[39m is described as [0m[32m"a wild pointer [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32minside of access range of size 0x000000000001"[0m[39m, suggesting a single-byte write [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperation to an invalid memory location.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Codebase Areas Requiring Investigation**:[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Primary Focus - `[0m[35m/src/FreeRDP/libfreerdp/crypto/[0m[95mcertificate.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m1570[0m[39m`**: The [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexact location where the buffer overflow write occurs in the [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`freerdp_bio_read_pem_with_policy` function. This function appears to be [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresponsible for reading PEM certificate data with policy validation.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Certificate Data Loading - [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/FreeRDP/libfreerdp/crypto/[0m[95mcertificate_data.c[0m[39m`**: Multiple functions in this [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfile are part of the call stack:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m84[0m[39m: `freerdp_certificate_data_load_cache`[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m126[0m[39m: `freerdp_certificate_data_new_nocopy`[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m155[0m[39m: `freerdp_certificate_data_new_from_pem`[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **PEM Processing - `[0m[35m/src/FreeRDP/libfreerdp/crypto/[0m[95mcertificate.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m1634[0m[39m`**: The [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`freerdp_certificate_get_pem_ex` function which calls the vulnerable function.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Buffer Allocation and Management**: Investigation should include how buffers [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare allocated, sized, and managed throughout the PEM certificate parsing process, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparticularly in the context of the functions identified in the call stack.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Input Validation**: The fuzzer was able to trigger this vulnerability, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msuggesting potential issues with input validation or bounds checking when [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing PEM certificate data. The testcase that triggered this issue should be [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39manalyzed to understand what specific input patterns cause the overflow.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability appears to be related to PEM certificate data processing, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecifically when loading and parsing certificate data from memory, with [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minsufficient bounds checking or incorrect buffer size calculations leading to the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap buffer overflow.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1517[0m[39m:   [0m[39mpem[0m[1;39m[[0m[39moffset[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1520[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m*plength = offset;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1524[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpem[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis Summary[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the code snippets and evaluation report, I've identified the root [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause and the optimal fix strategy:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Root Cause:**[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe `freerdp_bio_read_pem_with_policy` function at [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/FreeRDP/libfreerdp/crypto/[0m[95mcertificate.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m1529[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1580[0m[39m` has a critical [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap-buffer-overflow vulnerability caused by:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Use of `uint16_t` for size variables [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`offset`, `length`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m which overflow after [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m~[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m iterations [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m65536[0m[39m [0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m2048[0m[39m = [0m[1;36m32[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Missing safety check after reading data to exit loop early when buffer is not [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompletely filled[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Incorrect loop condition `while [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstatus != [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` instead of `while [0m[1;39m([0m[39moffset < [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is triggered when:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A certificate with Extended Validation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mEV[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m policy OID [0m[32m"2.23.140.1.2.1"[0m[39m is [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessed[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The certificate or certificate chain is large enough to require more than [0m[1;36m65535[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The function attempts to read the PEM data using uint16_t variables, causing [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minteger overflow[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Critical Observations:**[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The codebase already contains a correct, safe implementation: `bio_read_pem` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1477[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1527[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The vulnerable function was added to handle EV certificates differently, but [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mironically, EV certificates are often larger and MORE likely to trigger the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Both functions are called from `freerdp_certificate_get_pem_ex` based on policy [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecking [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1633[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1637[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix: Replace Vulnerable Implementation with Safe Pattern[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location:** `[0m[35m/src/FreeRDP/libfreerdp/crypto/[0m[95mcertificate.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m1529[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1580[0m[39m`[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Changes Required:**[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Change variable types from `uint16_t` to `size_t`** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1537[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1539[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change `const uint16_t blocksize = [0m[1;36m2048[0m[39m;` to `const size_t blocksize = [0m[1;36m2048[0m[39m;`[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change `uint16_t offset = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;` to `size_t offset = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;`[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change `uint16_t length = blocksize;` to `size_t length = blocksize;`[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Update loop condition** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1546[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change `while [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstatus != [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to `while [0m[1;39m([0m[39moffset < length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This provides an additional safety check to prevent offset from exceeding [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated size[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Change status variable initialization** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1532[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change `int status = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m;` to make it local within the loop [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlike in [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`bio_read_pem`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Alternatively, keep it but don't rely on it for loop continuation[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Add critical safety check after reading** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter line [0m[1;36m1566[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add the following check immediately after `offset += [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mstatus;`:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength - offset > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       break;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This ensures the loop exits after a partial read, preventing unnecessary [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer growth and ensuring offset stays within bounds[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Move length increment** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1567[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keep `length += blocksize;` but ensure it only executes when the buffer was [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompletely filled[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - With the safety check in step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m, this naturally happens only when needed[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Detailed Implementation Steps[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Update variable declarations [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1537[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1539[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconst uint16_t blocksize = [0m[1;36m2048[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muint16_t offset = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWith:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Update loop structure [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1546[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1569[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstatus != [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    char* tmp = [0m[1;35mrealloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpem, length + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!tmp[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        goto fail;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    pem = tmp;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mERR_clear_error[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    status = [0m[1;35mBIO_read[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbio, &pem[0m[1;39m[[0m[39moffset[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength - offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstatus < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mWLog_ERR[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTAG, [0m[32m"failed to read certificate"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstatus == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        break;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile [0m[1;39m([0m[39moffset < length[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    pem = tmp;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mERR_clear_error[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    const int status = [0m[1;35mBIO_read[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbio, &pem[0m[1;39m[[0m[39moffset[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength - offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstatus < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mWLog_ERR[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTAG, [0m[32m"failed to read certificate"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        goto fail;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstatus == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        break;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    offset += [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mstatus;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength - offset > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        break;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    length += blocksize;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Key changes in Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m:**[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Loop condition: `while [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstatus != [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → `while [0m[1;39m([0m[39moffset < length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Make `status` local: `int status = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m;` declaration outside loop → `const int [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstatus` inside loop[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add safety check: Insert `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength - offset > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break;` after offset update[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This matches the proven safe pattern from `bio_read_pem`[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Remove or update status variable declaration [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1532[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSince status is now declared inside the loop, remove the declaration at line [0m[1;36m1532[0m[39m:[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mint status = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Remove this line[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Fix is Optimal[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Proven Pattern**: This fix applies the exact same pattern used successfully in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`bio_read_pem` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1477[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1527[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which has been handling certificates correctly [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout issues.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Minimal Changes**: The fix only modifies the vulnerable function, preserving [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mall existing functionality and call sites. No changes to:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `freerdp_certificate_get_pem_ex` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe caller[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `freerdp_certificate_policies` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe policy checker[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Certificate parsing/loading logic[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Test code or fuzzing harness[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Root Cause Resolution**: Addresses both critical issues:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Integer overflow: `size_t` can handle certificates of any realistic size [0m[1;39m([0m[39mup [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto platform limits[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Buffer overrun: Safety check ensures offset never exceeds allocated buffer [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Preserves Intended Functionality**: The function still:[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Reads PEM data from BIO in chunks[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Dynamically grows buffer as needed[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Handles end-of-data correctly[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Null-terminates the result[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Returns length via output parameter[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **No Side Effects**: The function signature and return behavior remain [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39midentical, so no changes needed in calling code.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Vulnerability[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Integer Overflow Prevention**: [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `size_t` on [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m-bit systems can hold values up to [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m^[0m[1;36m64[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;36m18[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m446[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m744[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m073[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m709[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m551[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m615[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Even massive certificate chains [0m[1;39m([0m[39m100KB+[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m won't cause overflow[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Prevents wraparound that caused incorrect buffer allocation[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Buffer Overrun Prevention**:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Loop condition `while [0m[1;39m([0m[39moffset < length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` prevents offset from exceeding [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated size[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Safety check `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength - offset > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break;` exits after partial reads[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensures `pem[0m[1;39m[[0m[39moffset[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m` at line [0m[1;36m1570[0m[39m always writes within bounds[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Buffer is always allocated as `length + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`, and offset is guaranteed ≤ length [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mafter loop[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Maintains Correctness**:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Reads all available data from BIO[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Grows buffer only when needed [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhen completely filled[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Handles EOF [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstatus == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m correctly[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Proper error handling with goto fail pattern[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Side Effects:** [0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m expected, because:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **API Compatibility**: Function signature unchanged, return values unchanged[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Behavior Preservation**: Still reads and returns PEM data identically[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Caller Expectations**: All callers [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`freerdp_certificate_get_pem_ex`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m expect [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe same behavior[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Memory Management**: Still uses realloc/free pattern consistently[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Testing Considerations:**[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fix should pass the existing fuzzer test that triggered the issue[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Should handle both small and large certificates correctly[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Should work for both EV and non-EV certificates[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The safety check ensures efficient memory usage [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno over-allocation[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Alternative Approaches Rejected[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Remove policy-specific path entirely**[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Could change line [0m[1;36m1633[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1637[0m[39m to always call `bio_read_pem`[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Rejected**: May break intended EV certificate handling logic; RFC [0m[1;36m7299[0m[39m comment [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msuggests policy-specific handling was intentional[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Increase uint16_t to uint32_t**[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Would delay overflow but not prevent it for very large chains[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Rejected**: Still has potential overflow; size_t is the proper type for sizes[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Add size check before calling function**[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Check BIO size before reading and reject if too large[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Rejected**: Arbitrary limits are bad practice; proper fix handles any size[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe `bio_read_pem` function at lines [0m[1;36m1477[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1527[0m[39m demonstrates this exact pattern is [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malready proven in production code. Other similar patterns in the codebase:[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All buffer management uses `size_t` for sizes[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- OpenSSL integration examples use `size_t` throughout[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Memory allocation patterns consistently use proper types[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix brings `freerdp_bio_read_pem_with_policy` in line with established [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcodebase practices and eliminates the vulnerability while maintaining full [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
